    "theoretical calculations @xcite , and a variety of experimental data @xcite support the assumption that the high-@xmath1 cuprates are characterized by dynamical stripe - like inhomogeneities , where narrow charged stripes form antiphase domain walls separating wider antiferromagnetic ( af ) stripes .",
    "experimental observations have been pointing to the presence of both itinerant and almost localized ( or polaron - like ) carriers in the cuprates .",
    "first - principles calculations @xcite support an approach based on the existence of both large-@xmath0 and small-@xmath0 orbitals in the vicinity of the fermi level ( @xmath2 ) .",
    "the fermion creation operator of a small-@xmath0 electron in band @xmath3 , spin @xmath4 ( which can be assigned a number @xmath5 ) , and wave vector @xmath6 is denoted here by @xmath7 .",
    "the creation operators of the large-@xmath0 electrons in the cuo@xmath8 planes are expressed using the `` slave - fermion '' method @xcite .",
    "such an electron in site @xmath9 and spin @xmath4 is created by @xmath10 , if it is in the `` upper - hubbard - band '' , and by @xmath11 , if it is in a zhang - rice - type `` lower - hubbard - band '' . here",
    "@xmath12 and @xmath13 are ( `` excession '' and `` holon '' ) fermion operators , and @xmath14 are ( `` spinon '' ) boson operators .",
    "these auxiliary operators have to satisfy the constraint : @xmath15 .",
    "further details on results presented here are given elsewhere @xcite .",
    "an auxiliary space is introduced within which a chemical - potential - like lagrange multiplier imposes the constraint on the average .",
    "the projection of observable quantities to the physical space is achieved by expressing them as combinations of green s functions of the auxiliary space , whose time evolution is determined by a hamiltonian obeying the constraint rigorously . thus it is expected to be maintained as long as justifiable approximations are used .    in the zeroth order",
    ", the spinon field is diagonalized by applying the bogoliubov transformation @xcite : @xmath16 .",
    "the `` bare '' spinons , created by @xmath17 , have energies @xmath18 with a v - shape zero minimum at @xmath19 .",
    "bose condensation results in af order at wave vector @xmath20 .",
    "along the one dimensional charged stripes the spin - charge separation approximation is expected to be valid .",
    "thus it is justified there to decouple two - particle spinon - holon ( spinon - excession ) green s functions into single - auxiliary - particle green s functions , and to interpret the auxiliary particles as physical quasiparticles .",
    "we refer to holons ( excessions ) along the charged stripes as `` stripons '' , created by @xmath21 , having bare energies by @xmath22 , and carrying charge @xmath23 .",
    "since the dynamical stripe - like inhomogeneities are highly disordered , we find it appropriate to assume zeroth order localized stripon states .",
    "their @xmath6 wavenumbers present @xmath6-symmetrized combinations of degenerate localized states to be treated in a perturbation expansion .",
    "their values are within a brillouin zone ( bz ) based on periodic supercells which are large enough to approximately contain ( each ) the entire spectrum @xmath24 of bare stripon energies .",
    "these supercells introduce an approximate long - range order in spite of the local inhomogeneities .",
    "we do not assume spin - charge separation away from the charged stripes , and construct approximate fermion creation operators of coupled holon - spinon and excession - spinon basis states as follows : @xmath25 where the index @xmath26 accounts for the structure of the unit cell , and : @xmath27 , @xmath28 , @xmath29 .",
    "the states created by @xmath30 and @xmath31 are orthogonalized to the stripon states , and depleted to avoid over - completeness .",
    "together with the small-@xmath0 states [ created by @xmath7 ] they form , within the auxiliary space , a basis to `` quasi - electron '' ( qe ) states whose creation operators are denoted by @xmath33 , and mean - field bare energies by @xmath34 .",
    "these energies form quasi - continuous ranges of bands within the bz around @xmath2 .",
    "the hopping and hybridization terms of the hamiltonian introduce strong coupling between the qe , stripon and spinon fields .",
    "this can be expressed through a coupling hamiltonian term whose parameters can be in principle derived self - consistently from the original hamiltonian . for the case of p - type cuprates",
    "this coupling hamiltonian can be expressed as : @xmath35 + h.c .",

    "@xmath36 introduces a vertex between the qe , stripon and spinon propagators @xcite .",
    "a localized stripon modifies the lattice around it @xcite .",
    "consequently , physical process induced by @xmath36 , in which a stripon is transformed into a qe , or vice versa , and a spinon is emitted and/or absorbed , involves also the emission and/or absorption of phonons .",
    "this can be described by multiplying a spinon propagator , linked to the @xmath36 vertex with a power series of phonon propagators @xcite",
    ". such a phonon-dressed \" spinon is referred to as a  svivon \" , carrying spin and lattice distortion , and the @xmath37 vertex is re - interpreted as coupling between a qe , stripon , and svivon propagators .",

    "the low - energy signature of the stripon spectral functions is not detected by spectroscopies , like arpes , which measure the effect of transfer of electrons into , or out of , the crystal .",
    "it is smeared over few tenths of an ev through convolution with svivon spectral functions , and contributes an `` incoherent '' background . on the other hand ,",
    "transport properties measure the electrons _ within _ the crystal , and can detect the stripon energy scale .",
    "the physical contribution of the quasi - continuum of qe bands to the electron spectral functions is strong only for few qe bands for which the expansion coefficients in terms of their basis states [ created by ( 1,2 ) @xmath59 , @xmath60 , and @xmath7 ] closely correspond to those of real electron states , and they contribute `` coherent '' @xmath61 bands .",
    "the other qe states also contribute to the incoherent background .",

    "the consequence of the logarithmic singularity in @xmath67 at @xmath68 [ due to the @xmath69 term in eq .",
    "( 13 ) ] , for p - type cuprates ( 16 ) , is that as an @xmath70 band approaches @xmath2 from below it is becoming flatter ( though it does not narrow accordingly ) while from above it becomes steeper , and may pass through an infinite slope resulting in an s - shape triply valued band ( causing smearing of the spectral weight , and blurring the band ) . the effect of the singularity is truncated and smoothened on an energy scale @xmath71ev . for",
    "`` real '' n - type cuprates these behaviors below and above @xmath2 are expected to switch .",
    "arpes data reflects the behavior below @xmath2 , and results of such band - flattening have been reported in p - type cuprates ( and attributed to electron coupling with phonons @xcite or with the neutron scattering resonance mode @xcite ) .",
    "the behavior above @xmath2 would be detected in aripes measurements .",
    "further measurements of the bands of n - type cuprates very close to @xmath2 are necessary to determine their behavior there",
    ".    the renormalization of svivon energies ( from @xmath72 to @xmath73 ) due to @xmath74 ( 15 ) , and specifically its logarithmic singularity at @xmath68 due to the @xmath75 term ( which is smoothened at low energies ) results in a negative shift close to the minimum at @xmath76 ; and as @xmath77 is approached , the slope of @xmath78 increases first [ compared to the almost constant slope of @xmath79 and it may become infinite , resulting in a range of an s - shape triply valued and blurred band ; but as @xmath77 is further approached , the slope of @xmath78 decreases and becomes smaller than the slope of @xmath80 at its minimum at @xmath77 . from analyticity arguments ( due to the absence of long - range af order )",
    "it is expected that @xmath78 has a smooth minimum , rather than the v - shape minimum of @xmath80 .",
    "thus @xmath81 presents the crossover energy from the intermediary to the low energy range .",
    "since spin - flip excitations are , largely , double - svivon absorption or emission processes , @xmath82 is expected to be the energy of such an excitation at @xmath83 .",
    "this result is consistent with the neutron - scattering resonance found at this wave number @xcite .",
    "it is observed that this resonance is at a local energy maximum , for @xmath84 around @xmath85 , consistently with our result that @xmath86 is at a minimum below zero .",
    "an anomalous optical conductivity has been observed for the high-@xmath1 cuprates @xcite , consisting of drude and mid - ir terms .",
    "this is consistent with our results , where the drude term is due to transitions between qe states , and between stripon states , while the mid - ir term largely results from transitions between stripon states and qe+svivon states .",
    "the mid - ir term becomes negligibly small for @xmath87 , where the conductivity could be decoupled into qe and stripon terms .",

1488,419.01 )    ' '' ''    ( 1488.00,418.51)(3.500,1.000)2    ' '' ''    the transport results in fig .  1 correspond to five stoichiometries , ranging from underdoped ( @xmath106 ) to overdoped ( @xmath107 ) p - type cuprates .",
    "the parameter @xmath108 , corresponding to the qe contribution to the electrons density of states at @xmath2 , is assumed to increase with doping , reflecting transfer of qe spectral weight towards @xmath2 .",
    "consequently ( 5 ) @xmath98 is assumed to decrease with doping .",
    "the parameters @xmath109 and @xmath110 represent effective qe and stripon contributions to the density of charge carriers ( reflected in the hall number ) .",
    "since they both contribute through the current @xmath111 of the bare qe states , they are expected to have same sign ( corresponding to these states ) .",
    "the values of these parameters are assumed to increase with doping , where @xmath110 increases considerably faster than @xmath109 , and a little faster than @xmath112 ( since @xmath110 reflects an overall stripon - related carriers density , while @xmath99 is the fractional occupation of stripon states within the charged stripes whose number increases with doping ) .",
    "doping - independent values are taken for the qe tep parameter @xmath113 [ which is negative for p - type cuprates by the inequality ( 16 ) ] , and for the stripon and qe scattering rate parameters @xmath114 , @xmath115 , @xmath116 , and @xmath117 .",
    "the tep results depend strongly on @xmath99 , and reproduce very well the doping - dependent experimental behavior @xcite .",
    "the position of the maximum in @xmath96 depends on the choice of @xmath98 , and it may occur below or above @xmath1 ( a pg may shift it to a higher temperature than predicted here ) . also the other transport coefficient in fig .  1",
    "reproduce very well the experimental behavior @xcite .",
    "cases where the linear @xmath50 dependence of the resistivity persists at very low temperatures are expected as a pg effect .",
    "the tep in `` real '' n - type cuprates is expected to behave similarly to p - type cuprates , but with an opposite sign and slope .",
    "results for ncco @xcite reveal that for doping levels where it is superconducting ( sc ) , the tep slope actually corresponds to those of p - type cuprates [ fig .",
    "1(a ) ] , but with an opposite effect of doping .",
    "thus @xmath96 for lower doping levels is typical of the p - type overdoped regime .",
    "this points to the possibility that ncco is not a `` real '' n - type cuprate , and its stripons are also based on holon states , where the extra doped negative charge occupies another qe band .",
    "the hall constant in ncco @xcite is also consistent with this scenario and our results .",
    "another possibility is that the tep slope in ncco is determined by electrons which are not strongly coupled to the cuo@xmath8 planes .",
    "the electronic structure of the cuprates discussed here provides sc pairing due to transitions between pair states of stripons and qe s through the exchange of svivons @xcite . since such transitions enable long - range hopping of local stripon pairs , without an associated hopping of svivons ( necessary for single - stripon hopping ) , this type of pairing results in a large gain in the `` kinetic '' energy of the stripons .",
    "thus this can effectively be expressed as a strong attractive stripon - stripon interaction .",
    "thus , pair - breaking is then expected to result in both qe and stripon+svivon excitations .",
    "this is confirmed by arpes results in the sc state @xcite , showing a sharp peak at @xmath118ev over a wide range of the bz , and a `` hump '' starting at @xmath119ev and merging with a normal - state band at higher energies , corresponding to these excitations .",
    "the hump is consistent with the qe pair - breaking excitation , and the peak with the stripon+svivon pair - breaking excitation at the svivon minimum @xmath86 . in the sc state",
    "this minimum is within the gap , and thus is considerably narrower than in the normal state [ reflected also in the width of the neutron - scattering resonance energy @xmath82 ] .",
    "when the pairing energy is comparable to the relevant bandwidth , a crossover is expected @xcite to occur between bcs and preformed - pairs bose - einstein condensation ( bec ) behaviors .",
    "this condition is fulfilled here due to the small stripon bandwidth , and the underdoped cuprates are characterized by bec behavior , where singlet pairs are formed at @xmath121 , and sc occurs below @xmath122 where phase coherence sets in .",
    "the normal - state pg is a pair - breaking gap at @xmath123 , having similarities to the sc gap , and accounting for most of the pairing energy , as observed @xcite .",
    "the coherence temperature can be expressed @xcite as : @xmath124 , where @xmath125 and @xmath126 are the pairs effective mass and density , in agreement with the `` uemura plots '' .",
    "since we expect [ fig .",
    "1(a ) ] the stripon band to be half full ( @xmath127 ) for slightly overdoped cuprates , the `` boomerang - type '' behavior @xcite of these plots is understood as a crossover between a stripon band - top @xmath128 behavior in the underdoped cuprates , and a stripon band - bottom @xmath129 behavior in overdoped cuprates .",
    "it was shown that a treatment of the cuprates on the basis of both large-@xmath0 and small-@xmath0 orbitals and dynamical stripe - like inhomogeneities resolves puzzling normal - state spectroscopic and transport properties and provides a mechanism for high-@xmath1 and the peudogap .",

    "<S> considering both `` large-@xmath0 '' and `` small-@xmath0 '' orbitals , it is found that the carriers of the high-@xmath1 cuprates are polaron - like `` stripons '' carrying charge and located on stripe - like inhomogeneities , `` quasi - electrons '' carrying charge and spin , and `` svivons '' carrying spin and lattice distortion . </S>",
    "<S> this is shown to result in the observed anomalous spectroscopic and transport properties of the cuprates . pairing results from transitions between pair states of stripons and quasi - electrons through the exchange of svivons , and </S>",
    "<S> a crossover occurs between bcs and bose - einstein condensation behaviors .    # </S>",
